### [227] [Beyond Accuracy: Policy Invariance as a Reliability Test for LLM Safety Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06161)
*Shihao Weng,Yang Feng,Xiaofei Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出当前 LLM-as-a-Judge 用于智能体安全评估时存在“策略措辞敏感性”问题，并提出政策不变性测试协议、Policy Invariance Score 与 Judge Card，用于审计评估器可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体安全基准通常把 LLM 评审器的裁决当作近似真值，但很少检验裁决是否真正取决于智能体行为，还是受评估策略提示词的表述方式影响。作者希望建立可信安全评审器应满足的基本性质。

Method: 作者提出 policy invariance，并将其操作化为三项可测试原则：语义等价改写下的 rubric-semantics invariance、有意严格到宽松变化下的 rubric-threshold invariance，以及使不稳定裁决集中于真实模糊样本的 ambiguity-aware calibration。基于 ASSEBench 和 R-Judge 的轨迹，对四类 agent-class judges 进行压力测试。

Result: 实验发现当前评审器对有意义的规范阈值变化与无意义的结构性改写反应强度相近，难以区分二者。保持内容不变的策略改写会导致最高 9.1% 的裁决翻转超过基线抖动，且在这些改写下 18–43% 的翻转发生在非模糊样本上。

Conclusion: 仅依赖准确率排行榜会掩盖评审器可靠性的巨大差异；评估智能体安全时必须同时审计评估器本身。作者提出的 Policy Invariance Score 与 Judge Card 可揭示不同评审器在策略不变性上的数量级差异，并为未来基准提供可复用审计协议。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-Judge pipelines have become the de facto evaluator for agent safety, yet existing benchmarks treat their verdicts as ground-truth proxies without checking whether the verdicts depend on the agent's behavior or merely on how the evaluation policy happens to be worded. We argue that any trustworthy safety judge must satisfy a basic property we call policy invariance, and we operationalize it as three testable principles: rubric-semantics invariance under certified-equivalent rewrites, rubric-threshold invariance under intentional strict-to-lenient shifts, and ambiguity-aware calibration so that verdict instability concentrates on genuinely ambiguous cases. Instantiating these principles as a stress-test protocol with four agent-class judges on trajectories drawn from ASSEBench and R-Judge, we surface a previously unmeasured failure mode: today's judges respond to meaningful normative shifts and to meaningless structural rewrites with comparable strength, and cannot tell the two apart. Content-preserving policy rewrites flip up to 9.1% of verdicts above baseline jitter, and 18-43% of all observed flips occur on unambiguous cases under such rewrites, so existing safety scores conflate what the agent did with how the evaluator was prompted. Beyond the diagnosis, we contribute the Policy Invariance Score and the Judge Card reporting protocol, which expose an order-of-magnitude spread in judge reliability that is invisible to accuracy-only leaderboards. We release the protocol and code so that future agent-safety benchmarks can audit their own evaluators rather than trust them by default.

Abstract: Building a deep research agent today is an exercise in glue code: the same backbone evaluated on the same benchmark can report different accuracies in different papers because harness and tool registry all differ, and integrating a new foundation model into a comparable evaluation surface costs weeks of model-specific engineering. We call this the per-paper engineering tax and release BioMedArena, an open-source toolkit that not only alleviates it but also provides an arena for fair comparison of different foundation models when evaluating them as deep-research agents. BioMedArena decouples six layers of biomedical agent evaluation -- benchmark loading, tool exposure, tool selection, execution mode, context management, and scoring -- and exposes 147 biomedical benchmarks and 75 biomedical tools across 9 functional families. Adding a new model, benchmark, or tool reduces to registering a few-line provider adapter. We further provide 6 agent harnesses with 6 context-management strategies, which provide 12 backbones with competitive research capabilities and significantly improved performance, achieving state-of-the-art (SOTA) results on 8 representative biomedical benchmarks, with an average lift of +15.03 percentage points over prior SOTA. ### [229] [Event-Causal RAG: A Retrieval-Augmented Generation Framework for Long Video Reasoning in Complex Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06185)
*Peizheng Yan,Yu Zhao,Liang Xie,Juntong Qi,Mingming Wang,Erwei Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Event-Causal RAG：将长视频流切分为语义事件，用状态-事件-状态（SES）图表示并构建全局事件知识图，通过语义与因果拓扑双重检索支持超长/无限视频推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大视觉语言模型在短中视频理解上表现较好，但面对超长甚至无限视频时难以维持长期一致记忆并推断远距离事件间因果关系；端到端方法受自注意力 O(n^2) 复杂度限制，现有 RAG 又存在片段记忆割裂、时序/因果结构建模弱、存储与在线推理成本高等问题。

Method: 方法不再索引固定长度视频片段，而是将流式视频分割为语义连贯事件；每个事件表示为结构化 SES 图，捕捉事件及其前后状态转移；多个 SES 图合并为全局事件知识图，并存入支持语义匹配和因果拓扑检索的双存储记忆；随后采用双向检索策略找出相关事件因果链及对应视频证据，输入骨干视频基础模型生成答案。

Result: 在长视频理解基准上，该框架相较强片段检索基线和长上下文视频模型表现更优，尤其在需要多事件整合和跨长时间间隔因果推理的问题上优势明显，同时具备更好的内存效率和流式鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Event-Causal RAG 通过事件级结构化记忆与因果链检索，为超长/无限视频理解提供了比片段级 RAG 和长上下文建模更高效、更具可解释性的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent large vision-language models have achieved strong performance on short- and medium-length video understanding, yet they remain inadequate for ultra-long or even infinite video reasoning, where models must preserve coherent memory over extended durations and infer causal dependencies across temporally distant events. Existing end-to-end video understanding methods are fundamentally limited by the $O(n^2)$ complexity of self-attention, while recent retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) approaches still suffer from fragmented clip-level memory, weak modeling of temporal and causal structure, and high storage and online inference costs. We present Event-Causal RAG, a lightweight retrieval-augmented framework for infinite long-video reasoning. Instead of indexing fixed-length clips, our method segments streaming videos into semantically coherent events and represents each event as a structured State-Event-State (SES) graph, capturing the event together with its surrounding state transitions. These graphs are merged into a global Event Knowledge Graph and stored in a dual-store memory that supports both semantic matching and causal-topological retrieval. On top of this memory, we design a bidirectional retrieval strategy to efficiently identify the most relevant event causal chains and provide them, together with the associated video evidence, to a backbone video foundation model for answer generation. Experiments on long-video understanding benchmarks demonstrate that Event-Causal RAG consistently outperforms strong clip-based retrieval baselines and long-context video models, particularly on questions requiring multi-event integration and causal inference across long temporal gaps, while also achieving improved memory efficiency and robust streaming performance.

</details>


### [230] [Systematic Evaluation of Large Language Models for Post-Discharge Clinical Action Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06191)
*Shivali Dalmia,Ananya Mantravadi,Prasanna Desikan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估零样本与少样本大语言模型在临床出院记录中抽取安全关键行动项的能力，发现LLM在二分类行动性检测上可媲美或超过监督模型，但在细粒度多标签分类上仍弱于任务特定监督模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 出院记录叙事复杂，过渡护理与出院后患者安全依赖准确识别可执行临床任务；同时，现有标注只给标签缺少理由，难以判断模型错误源于临床推理不足还是标注规范不一致。

Method: 使用CLIP discharge-note数据集，提出两阶段提示式抽取框架：先分解叙事型出院记录，再抽取细粒度、明确可执行的临床任务；系统比较生成式LLM的零/少样本表现、通用LLM与监督式BERT类任务模型，并分析不同动作类别的标注不一致。

Result: 当代LLM在二元行动性检测任务上达到或超过监督基线；但在细粒度多标签类别分类中，监督BERT类模型仍具有明显优势。定性错误分析显示，许多错误来自模型推理与数据集标注惯例之间的不匹配，尤其涉及隐式临床行动和严格结构化标签规则。

Conclusion: 单纯标签无法充分评估模型的临床理解，报告性能混合了模型能力限制与标注规范偏差。临床NLP需要带有推理依据的标注数据集，说明为何某些文本片段是可行动的，从而更准确地区分临床推理失败与标注约定不匹配。

Abstract: The work in this paper evaluates zero-shot and few-shot large language models (LLMs) for safety-critical clinical action extraction using the CLIP discharge-note dataset, with particular emphasis on transitions of care and post-discharge patient safety. To manage the complexity of clinical documentation, we introduce a two-stage extraction framework that decomposes discharge notes, that are written in narrative form, into fine-grained, explicitly actionable clinical tasks through a staged prompting strategy. Our contributions include a systematic assessment of generative LLMs for clinical action extraction, a detailed comparison between general-purpose LLMs and task-specific supervised BERT-based models, and an analysis of annotation inconsistencies across different action categories. We show that contemporary LLMs achieve performance comparable to or exceeding supervised models on binary actionability detection, while supervised baselines retain a meaningful advantage on fine-grained multi-label category classification, despite the absence of task-specific fine-tuning and under strict data-privacy constraints. Qualitative error analysis reveals that many failures stem from misalignment between model reasoning and dataset annotation conventions, particularly in cases involving implicit clinical actions and rigid structural labeling rules. These results indicate that reported performance reflects model limitations due to lack of clinical reasoning, that is not captured by plain annotations. Labels without rationales make it impossible to distinguish clinical reasoning failures from annotation convention mismatches. Advancing clinical NLP requires reasoning-annotated datasets that document why specific spans are actionable, not merely which spans were labeled, enabling proper evaluation of model clinical understanding.

### [231] [Towards Annotation-Free Validation of MLLMs: A Vision-Language Logical Consistency Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06201)
*Ying Gu,Mei Chee Leong,Hui Li Tan,Shangbo Mao,Liyuan Li,Nancy Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需真实标注即可评估多模态大语言模型视觉-语言逻辑一致性的指标VL-LCM，发现现有模型虽准确率提升明显，但逻辑一致性仍显著不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统准确率评估可能奖励模型的无依据猜测，并且在缺乏真实答案标注的新任务中难以用于模型验证。因此，需要一种能衡量模型回答是否符合基本逻辑、且可在无gt标注场景中使用的评估方法。

Method: 作者基于充分条件与必要条件的因果逻辑关系，构建视觉-语言逻辑一致性评估框架，并在传统多选视觉问答测试及NaturalBench等无需真实标注的测试中定义VL-LCM指标；随后在MMMU、NaturalBench等基准上评估来自4个前沿模型家族的11个开源MLLM。

Result: 实验显示，尽管近期MLLM在准确率上已有较大进步，但其逻辑一致性明显滞后。作者还通过与基于gt的指标相关性、LCM可靠性以及VL-LCM与响应分布关系等分析，验证了VL-LCM的有效性与适用性。

Conclusion: 逻辑一致性可作为准确率之外的重要评估维度，用于衡量模型可靠性，并可在无真实标注的新任务中支持MLLM选择、验证和答案可信性论证。

Abstract: Dominant accuracy evaluation might reward unwarranted guessing of Large Language Models, and it might not be applicable to novel tasks for model validation without ground-truth (gt) annotation. Based on basic logic principle, we propose a novel framework to evaluate the vision-language logical consistency of MLLMs on both sufficient and necessary cause-effect relations. We define Vision-Language Logical Consistency Metric (VL-LCM) on traditional MC-VQA tests, and recent NaturalBench tests without the need for gt annotation. Through systematic experiments on representative VL benchmark MMMU and recent VL challenges like NaturalBench, we evaluated 11 recent open-source MLLMs from 4 frontier families. Our findings reveal that, despite significant progress of recent MLLMs on accuracy, logical consistency lags behind significantly. Extensive evaluations on the correlations of VL-LCM with metrics on gt, the reliability of LCM, and the relation of VL-LCM with response distribution justify the validity and applicability of VL-LCM even without gt annotation. Our findings suggest that, beyond accuracy, logical consistency could be employed for both accuracy and reliability. VL-LCM can also be employed for MLLM selection, validation, and reliable answer justification in novel tasks without gt annotation.

### [232] [Beyond Fixed Benchmarks and Worst-Case Attacks: Dynamic Boundary Evaluation for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06213)
*Haoxiang Wang,Da Yu,Huishuai Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出动态边界评估（DBE），通过寻找模型在单题通过概率约为0.5的能力边界，缓解固定基准的天花板/地板效应，并将不同模型放到统一难度—能力尺度上比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型评测多依赖固定题集，对所有模型使用相同样本，容易导致强模型饱和、弱模型过难，从而掩盖真实能力差异。作者认为最有信息量的评估点位于模型“刚好可能成功或失败”的边界区域。

Method: DBE包含三部分：构建经9个参考LLM验证并标注难度的校准题库；提出仅需API查询访问的Skill-Guided Boundary Search（SGBS）来为目标模型搜索边界题目；设计可将新模型映射到统一能力尺度、并在题库覆盖不足时自适应扩展评测集的协议。实验覆盖拒答安全性、过度拒答、受约束指令遵循、多轮谄媚抵抗等类别。

Result: 该方法在安全、能力、真实性相关任务上实现了更宽模型谱系的覆盖，减少了评测饱和问题，同时保持与现有数据集的兼容性。

Conclusion: DBE提供了一种比固定基准更具诊断性的LLM评估框架，能够围绕模型能力边界进行动态测量，并支持跨模型的统一尺度比较。

Abstract: Evaluating large language models (LLMs) today rests on fixed benchmarks that apply the same set of items to any model, producing ceiling and floor effects that mask capability gaps. We argue that the most informative evaluation signal lies at the boundary, where the per-prompt pass probability is near $0.5$ under random-sampling decoding, and propose Dynamic Boundary Evaluation (DBE), which actively locates each model's boundary and places it on a globally comparable difficulty scale. DBE delivers three artifacts: (i) a calibrated item bank covering safety, capability, and truthfulness, with per-item difficulty labels validated across $9$ reference LLMs; (ii) Skill-Guided Boundary Search (SGBS), a search algorithm that finds boundary items for a given target LLM using only API-level query access; and (iii) an evaluation protocol that places a new LLM on a unified ability scale and grows the evaluation set adaptively when the target falls outside the bank's coverage. We instantiate DBE on four categories spanning safety (harmful request refusal and over-refusal), capability (constrained instruction following), and truthfulness (multi-turn sycophancy resistance). The resulting evaluation covers a broader model spectrum without saturation while remaining compatible with existing datasets.

### [233] [Proactive Instance Navigation with Comparative Judgment for Ambiguous User Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06223)
*Junhyuk Kwon,Seungjoon Lee,Hyejin Park,Kyle Min,Jungseul Ok*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 ProCompNav：先构建候选目标池，再通过能区分候选的二元比较式提问逐步排除干扰项，从而在实例级导航中更准确、更省用户输入地定位目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言实例导航中，用户初始请求常不足以唯一指定目标。现有方法要么过早锁定首个 plausible 候选，要么虽收集多个候选但提问基于单个候选属性，无法有效区分候选池中的相似干扰项，导致决策过早、交互冗长且成功率受限。

Method: 提出两阶段框架 Proactive Instance Navigation with Comparative Judgment（ProCompNav）。第一阶段构建候选实例池；第二阶段进行比较式判断：每轮从当前候选池中抽取可分裂候选集合的属性-取值对，生成是/否问题，并一次性剪除所有与用户回答不一致的候选，将消歧转化为池级判别式提问。

Result: 在 CoIN-Bench 上，ProCompNav 在相同最小输入条件下相较交互式基线提升 Success Rate，也优于使用详细描述的非交互式基线，同时显著降低 Response Length。在 TextNav 上也取得 state-of-the-art Success Rate。

Conclusion: 比较式候选池判别提问能有效减少用户负担并提升实例级导航成功率，尤其适用于存在相似干扰项且初始请求不充分的自然语言导航场景。

Abstract: Natural-language instance navigation becomes challenging when the initial user request does not uniquely specify the target instance. A practical agent should reduce the user's burden by actively asking only the information needed to distinguish the target from similar distractors, rather than requiring a detailed description upfront. Existing approaches often fall short of this goal: they may stop at the first plausible candidate before sufficiently exploring alternatives, or, even after collecting multiple candidates, ask about the target's attributes derived from individual candidates rather than questions selected to distinguish candidates in the pool. As a result, despite the dialogue, the agent may still fail to distinguish the target from distractors, leading to premature decisions and lengthy user responses. We propose Proactive Instance Navigation with Comparative Judgment (ProCompNav), a two-stage framework that first constructs a candidate pool and then identifies the target through comparative judgment. At each round, ProCompNav extracts an attribute-value pair that splits the current pool, asks a binary yes/no question, and prunes all inconsistent candidates at once. This reframes disambiguation from open-ended target description to pool-level discriminative questioning, where each question is chosen to narrow the candidate set. On CoIN-Bench, ProCompNav improves Success Rate over interactive baselines with the same minimal input and non-interactive baselines with detailed descriptions, while substantially reducing Response Length. ProCompNav also achieves state-of-the-art Success Rate on TextNav, suggesting that comparative judgment is broadly useful for instance-level navigation among similar distractors.

</details>

Hygieia features a router-based and knowledge-enhanced framework that mitigates hallucination and tailors diagnostic strategies to different disease categories. Notably, it prioritizes risk-related genomic factors for rare diseases and provides confidence scores to assist clinical decision-making. We conducted a comprehensive evaluation demonstrating that Hygieia achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple diagnostic benchmarks. In collaboration with clinical experts from Yale School of Medicine and Duke-NUS Medical School, we further validated its practical utility by showing (1) Hygieia's superior diagnostic performance compared to physicians with an improvement from 12%-60% and (2) its effectiveness in assisting clinicians with medical records for handling real-world cases. ### [235] [Price of Fairness in Short-Term and Long-Term Algorithmic Selections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06227)
*Shahin Jabbari,Chen Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究序贯选择中的公平性与效用权衡，指出静态公平约束可能加剧长期差异，而简单投资型策略可在较低公平代价下缓解长期差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 既有公平性研究多集中于静态决策，但高风险场景中的算法决策会随时间改变群体分布；近期研究表明，静态公平约束可能在长期造成更大不平等，因此需要分析短期公平、长期公平与效用之间的动态关系。

Method: 作者构建一个风格化的序贯选择模型：决策者反复选择个体，选择同时影响即时效用与未来总体分布。在该框架下定义短期与长期的群体公平概念，并用公平代价（Price of Fairness, PoF）理论刻画公平约束相对于最优效用的损失；同时通过合成数据和真实数据进行实证验证。

Result: 理论上，作者刻画了短期最优策略与公平策略，并证明即使不同群体分布几乎相同，短期公平约束的PoF仍可能很大。相对地，长期差异可在简单投资策略下逐渐消失，且这些策略具有较低PoF。实验结果支持上述理论观察。

Conclusion: 论文表明，公平性不能仅以静态或短期指标衡量；在动态决策系统中，短期公平可能带来较高效用损失甚至不利长期结果，而面向长期分布改善的投资策略更可能同时实现较低代价和长期公平。

Abstract: Algorithmic decision-making in high-stakes settings can have profound impacts on individuals and populations. While much prior work studies fairness in static settings, recent results show that enforcing static fairness constraints may exacerbate long-run disparities. Motivated by this tension, we study a stylized sequential selection problem in which a decision-maker repeatedly selects individuals, affecting both immediate utility and the population distribution over time. We introduce notions of group fairness for both the short and long term and theoretically analyze the trade-off between fairness and utility via the Price of Fairness (PoF). We characterize optimal and fair policies in the short term and show that the PoF can be large even when group distributions are nearly identical. In contrast, we show that long-term disparities can vanish under simple investment policies that achieve a low PoF. We also empirically validate these theoretical observations using both synthetic and real datasets.

Abstract: As large models evolve from conversational assistants into autonomous agents, challenges increasingly arise from long-horizon decision making, tool use, and real environment interaction. Existing agenticinfrastructure remain fragmented across evaluation, data management, and agent evolution, making it difficult to discover risks systematically and improve models in a continuous closed loop. In this report, we present \textbf{Safactory}, a scalable agent factory for trustworthy autonomous intelligence. ### [237] [Data Language Models: A New Foundation Model Class for Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06290)
*Eda Erol,Giuliano Pezzoli,Ozer Cem Kelahmet*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 Data Language Model（DLM）作为面向表格数据的原生基础模型，并发布 Schema-1；其目标是在无需序列化或预处理的情况下直接理解原始单元格值，在多类表格任务上优于传统方法、AutoML 和现有表格基础模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本、图像、音频等主要模态已有原生基础模型，但表格数据仍依赖特征工程、编码、清洗、序列化等预处理流程。作者认为现有梯度提升树、AutoML、表格基础模型并未真正把表格作为一种原生模态来理解，因此需要一种可直接消费原始表格数据的基础模型层。

Method: 作者提出 DLM 概念，并实现首个模型 Schema-1。该模型含 1.4 亿参数，在超过 230 万个合成与真实表格数据集上训练，直接从原始单元格值学习表格内部结构、分布几何与跨列/跨行关系，用于行级预测、缺失值重建和数据集行业领域识别等任务。

Result: 摘要称 Schema-1 在既定行级预测基准上超过梯度提升集成、AutoML 栈和被评估的表格基础模型；在缺失值重建中，其平均重建误差低于经典统计方法和前沿大语言模型；还能仅基于原始单元格值识别未见数据集所属行业领域，而作者称此前表格模型无法完成该任务。

Conclusion: 本文主张 DLM 是 AI 技术栈中缺失的原生表格理解层，可减少或消除传统表格建模前的预处理管线，并为后续 AI 模型、智能体和垂直应用提供统一的表格数据基础能力。

Abstract: Every major data modality now has a foundation model that understands it natively: text has language models, images have vision models, audio has audio models. Tabular data, the modality on which many consequential real-world AI decisions are made, does not. Every approach to tabular AI today, from gradient-boosted trees to the latest tabular foundation models, requires a preprocessing pipeline before any model can consume the data. None of them understand tabular data as a modality. We introduce the Data Language Model (DLM), the missing foundation model for tabular data. A DLM understands tables the way a language model understands sentences: natively, without serialization or preprocessing, directly from raw cell values. It is the tabular data layer on which AI models, agents, and vertical AI applications can be built, eliminating the preprocessing pipelines that currently stand between raw data and every AI system that consumes it. We present Schema-1, the first DLM: a 140M parameter model trained on more than 2.3M synthetic and real-world tabular datasets. Schema-1 outperforms gradient-boosted ensembles, AutoML stacks, and the tabular foundation models we evaluate on established row-level prediction benchmarks. On missing value reconstruction it achieves lower reconstruction error than all classical statistical methods and frontier large language models on mean performance across conditions, establishing that structural understanding of a dataset's own distributional geometry is more useful for imputation than world knowledge encoded in language. It identifies the industry sector of any unseen dataset from raw cell values alone, reliably across any domain, a task no prior tabular model can perform. It is the native tabular understanding layer that has been missing from the AI stack.

</details>


### [238] [Addressing Labelled Data Scarcity: Taxonomy-Agnostic Annotation of PII Values in HTTP Traffic using LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06305)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Automated privacy audits of web and mobile applications often analyse outbound HTTP traffic to detect Personally Identifiable Information (PII) leakage. However, existing learning-based detectors typically depend on scarce, manually labelled traffic and are tightly coupled to fixed label taxonomies, limiting transferability across domains and evolving definitions of PII. This paper investigates whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can support taxonomy-agnostic annotation of explicitly transmitted PII values in HTTP message bodies when the taxonomy is provided at runtime. We introduce a multi-stage LLM-based pipeline that combines deterministic pre-processing with label-level classification, targeted instance-level value annotation, and output validation. To enable controlled evaluation and exemplar-based prompting without relying on sensitive real-user captures, we further propose an LLM-based generator for synthetic HTTP traffic with manually validated, taxonomy-derived PII annotations. We evaluate the approach across three taxonomies spanning different PII domains and granularity levels. Results show that the pipeline accurately detects PII types and extracts corresponding values for concrete PII taxonomies. Overall, our findings position LLMs as a promising foundation for flexible, taxonomy-agnostic traffic annotation and for creating labelled data under evolving privacy taxonomies.

### [239] [Rethinking Vacuity for OOD Detection in Evidential Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06382)
*Claire McNamara*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该摘要指出，EDL 中常用的 vacuity/不确定性质量指标对类别数 K 高度敏感；若 ID 与 OOD 的类别数不一致，AUROC/AUPR 可能在模型预测不变的情况下被人为抬高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 EDL 的 OOD 检测常使用 UM=K/S 衡量不确定性，但该指标直接依赖类别数 K。实践中，ID 与 OOD 数据的类别数未必被严格控制一致，可能导致评估结果混入类别基数差异带来的伪效应。

Method: 作者从理论上分析 UM 对 K 与总证据强度 S 的依赖关系，并通过经验实验比较 ID 与 OOD 类别数仅相差 1 时，标准 EDL 与 IB-EDL 在 AUROC、AUPR 指标上的变化；同时讨论该问题在基于 MCQA 数据集评估 EDL 微调大语言模型时的影响。

Result: 实验显示，当 ID 与 OOD 的类别数不同，即使模型预测没有变化，AUROC/AUPR 也可能显著变化：标准 EDL 中 AUROC 最大差异 0.318、AUPR 最大差异 0.613；IB-EDL 中 AUROC 最大差异 0.360、AUPR 最大差异 0.683。

Conclusion: 论文认为，基于 vacuity 的 EDL OOD 检测在 EDL 微调 LLM 场景下对类别基数控制非常敏感；若不确保 ID 与 OOD 的 K 一致，OOD 检测性能可能被评估伪影误导，因此需要更清晰地定义 ID/OOD 并控制类别数。

Abstract: Vacuity, or Uncertainty Mass (UM), is commonly used as a metric to evaluate Out-of-Distribution (OOD) detection in Evidential Deep Learning (EDL). It generally involves dividing the number of classes ($K$) by the total strength of belief ($S$) of the model's predictions, where $S$ is derived from summing the Dirichlet parameters. As such, UM is sensitive to the cardinality of $K$. In particular, it is unlikely in practice that there is a linear relationship between $K$ and $S$ as $K$ and $S$ increase due to the nature of EDL (suppressing incorrectly assigned evidence). As a result, when comparing In Distribution (ID) and OOD results, it is important that $K_{\mathrm{ID}}$ and $K_{\mathrm{OOD}}$ are equal; something that is not always ensured in practice. We provide an empirical demonstration of how results for AUROC and AUPR can substantially differ when class cardinality between ID and OOD differs by 1, with AUROC differing by as much as 0.318 and AUPR by 0.613 for standard EDL, and AUROC by 0.360 and AUPR by 0.683 for IB-EDL. More concretely, our findings isolate an evaluation artefact: when K differs between ID and OOD, AUROC/AUPR can be artificially inflated without any change in model predictions. We further discuss the evaluation of EDL over causal language models using Multiple-Choice Question-Answer (MCQA) datasets and argue for clearer definitions of ID and OOD in this context. Our primary contribution is an empirical and theoretical demonstration that vacuity-based OOD detection in EDL-fine-tuned LLMs is highly sensitive to uncontrolled differences in evaluated class cardinality.

</details>


### [240] [Knowledge Graphs, the Missing Link in Agentic AI-based Formal Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06434)
*Vaisakh Naduvodi Viswambharan,Keerthan Kopparam Radhakrishna,Deepak Narayan Gadde,Aman Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于验证中心知识图谱的多智能体流程，用于从自然语言规格和RTL/工具反馈中生成并迭代优化SystemVerilog Assertions，提升规格到RTL的语义对齐、可编译性与形式覆盖率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从规格、RTL以及形式工具反馈中抽取结构化中间表示，构建包含需求、设计层级、信号、假设、属性、语法诊断、反例和覆盖报告的验证知识图谱；多智能体查询并更新该图谱，执行SVA生成、基于诊断的语法修复、基于反例的语义纠错和基于覆盖的属性增强。

Result: 在七个基准设计上，知识图谱上下文检索改善了规格到RTL的grounding，稳定生成可编译SVA，且语法修复开销较低；形式覆盖率达到78.5%至99.4%。

Conclusion: 结构化IR与知识图谱能为LLM断言生成提供可追踪、设计扎根的上下文，显著提升SVA合成质量；但复杂时序和算术推理仍受当前LLM能力限制，收敛效果具有设计依赖性。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled workflows that generate SystemVerilog Assertions (SVAs) from natural-language specifications, with the potential to accelerate Formal Verification (FV). However, high-quality assertion synthesis remains challenging because specifications are often ambiguous or incomplete and critical micro-architectural details reside in the Register Transfer Level (RTL). Many existing approaches treat the specification and RTL as loosely structured text, which weakens specification-to-RTL grounding and leads to semantic mismatches and frequent syntax failures during formal parsing and elaboration. This work addresses these limitations with a verification-centric Knowledge Graph (KG) constructed from structured Intermediate Representations (IRs) extracted from the specification, RTL, and formal-tool feedback, including syntax diagnostics, Counterexamples (CEXs), and coverage reports. The KG links requirements, design hierarchy, signals, assumptions, and properties to provide traceable, design-grounded context for generation. A multi-agent workflow queries and updates this KG to generate SVAs and to drive three refinement loops: syntax repair guided by tool diagnostics, CEX-guided correction using trace links, and coverage-directed property augmentation. Evaluation across seven benchmark designs indicates that KG-based context retrieval improves specification-to-RTL grounding and consistently produces compilable SVAs with low syntax-repair overhead. The approach achieves formal coverage ranging from 78.5% to 99.4%, though convergence exhibits design dependence with complex temporal and arithmetic reasoning remaining challenging for current LLM capabilities.

</details>


### [241] [PrefixGuard: From LLM-Agent Traces to Online Failure-Warning Monitors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06455)
*Xinmiao Huang,Jinwei Hu,Rajarshi Roy,Changshun Wu,Yi Dong,Xiaowei Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PrefixGuard 是一种面向长程、工具使用型 LLM agent 的在线前缀风险监控框架，通过离线 StepView 归纳将原始异构轨迹转换为确定性类型化步骤，再训练轻量监督监控器进行早期风险预警；实验显示其整体优于原始文本基线与部署时 LLM judge，但不同任务的可操作预警能力存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM agent 执行长任务时，最终结果检查往往太晚，难以及时干预；在线预警需要轻量、可部署、能处理异构轨迹的前缀监控器，而人工事件模式脆弱，在线调用 LLM judge 成本高且效果有限。

Method: 提出 PrefixGuard：先离线使用 StepView 从原始轨迹样本中归纳确定性 typed-step adapter，将轨迹转为结构化步骤；再基于终端成败标签训练监督式监控器，学习事件抽象与前缀风险评分。还进行 observability ceiling 分析、DFA 后验抽取和 first-alert 诊断。

Conclusion: PrefixGuard 提供了一条实用的 monitor synthesis 路线：以离线结构化归纳降低部署成本，以监督训练实现前缀风险排序，并通过可观测性上界、DFA 审计和 first-alert 诊断判断预警是否真正可操作。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents now execute long, tool-using tasks where final outcome checks can arrive too late for intervention. Online warning requires lightweight prefix monitors over heterogeneous traces, but hand-authored event schemas are brittle and deployment-time LLM judging is costly. We introduce PrefixGuard, a trace-to-monitor framework with an offline StepView induction step followed by supervised monitor training. StepView induces deterministic typed-step adapters from raw trace samples, and the monitor learns an event abstraction and prefix-risk scorer from terminal outcomes. Across WebArena, $τ^2$-Bench, SkillsBench, and TerminalBench, the strongest PrefixGuard monitors reach 0.900/0.710/0.533/0.557 AUPRC. Using the strongest backend within each representation, they improve over raw-text controls by an average of +0.137 AUPRC. LLM judges remain substantially weaker under the same prefix-warning protocol. We also derive an observability ceiling on score-based area under the precision-recall curve (AUPRC) that separates monitor error from failures lacking evidence in the observed prefix. For finite-state audit, post-hoc deterministic finite automaton (DFA) extraction remains compact on WebArena and $τ^2$-Bench (29 and 20 states) but expands to 151 and 187 states on SkillsBench and TerminalBench. Finally, first-alert diagnostics show that strong ranking does not imply deployment utility: WebArena ranks well yet fails to support low-false-alarm alerts, whereas $τ^2$-Bench and TerminalBench retain more actionable early alerts. Together, these results position PrefixGuard as a practical monitor-synthesis recipe with explicit diagnostics for when prefix warnings translate into actionable interventions.

Applied to the Hierarchical Multi-Agent System for Payments (HMASP) across 18 LLMs and 90,000 task instances, ASR reveals that 10 of 18 models systematically skip a confirmation checkpoint during payment checkout, a deviation invisible to both TSR and HF1, while 8 models enforce the checkpoint perfectly. Notably, GPT-4.1 exhibits hidden workflow shortcuts despite achieving perfect TSR and HF1, while GPT-5.2 achieves perfect ASR. ### [243] [ReasonSTL: Bridging Natural Language and Signal Temporal Logic via Tool-Augmented Process-Rewarded Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06483)
*Bowen Ye,Zhijian Li,Junyue Huang,Junkai Ma,Xiang Yin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: STL 广泛用于自治系统和信息物理系统的验证与综合，但实际用户常以自然语言表达需求。人工编写 STL 需要专业知识且难以规模化；调用商业大模型 API 成本高，并可能泄露敏感系统需求。因此，需要一种低成本、可本地部署、隐私友好且可靠的自然语言到 STL 翻译方法。

Method: 论文提出 ReasonSTL，将翻译过程分解为显式推理、确定性工具调用和结构化公式构造；同时引入过程奖励训练，用于监督工具使用轨迹和最终 STL 公式。作者还构建 STL-Bench，一个双语、计算感知、基于真实信号的基准数据集，用于评估模型能力。

Abstract: Signal Temporal Logic (STL) is an expressive formal language for specifying spatio-temporal requirements over real-valued, real-time signals. It has been widely used for the verification and synthesis of autonomous systems and cyber-physical systems. In practice, however, users often express their requirements in natural language rather than in structured STL formulas, making natural-language-to-STL translation a critical yet challenging task. Manual specification requires temporal-logic expertise and cannot scale, while prompting commercial LLM APIs incurs substantial token costs and may expose sensitive system requirements to third-party services, raising privacy concerns for industrial deployment. To address these challenges, we present \textsc{ReasonSTL}, a tool-augmented framework that adapts local open-source language models for natural-language-to-STL generation. \textsc{ReasonSTL} decomposes the translation process into explicit reasoning, deterministic tool calls, and structured formula construction. We further introduce process-rewarded training to supervise both tool-use trajectories and final formulas, together with \textsc{STL-Bench}, a bilingual, computation-aware benchmark grounded in real-world signals. Experiments show that a 4B model trained with \textsc{ReasonSTL} achieves state-of-the-art performance in both automatic metrics and human evaluations, demonstrating that \textsc{ReasonSTL} provides a transparent, low-cost, and privacy-preserving alternative for formal specification drafting.

### [244] [From Token Lists to Graph Motifs: Weisfeiler-Lehman Analysis of Sparse Autoencoder Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06494)
*Ruben Fernandez-Boullon,Pablo Magariños-Docampo,Javier Perez-Robles*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 为每个 SAE 特征构造 token 共现图：节点为强激活附近最频繁出现的 token，边表示 token 对在局部上下文窗口内共现；随后设计 WL-style、基于频率分箱的图核来计算图结构相似度，并对来自 GPT-2 Small 上大型 SAE 的特征进行聚类，与解码器余弦相似度和 token-histogram 基线比较。

Result: 该方法在合成混合领域语料上的概念验证中恢复了若干启发式 motif 家族，如标点密集模式、语言/文字系统簇和代码式模板；这些结构簇无法通过解码器余弦相似度聚类得到。token-histogram 基线整体纯度更高，但图视角能揭示互补结构信息；聚类结果对图构造超参数和随机种子较稳定。

Conclusion: 论文的主要贡献不是全面优于频率基线，而是证明共现图表示可作为 SAE 特征分析的互补工具，捕捉 token 频率与解码器权重难以表达的高阶结构关系。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have become central to mechanistic interpretability, decomposing transformer activations into monosemantic features. Yet existing analyses characterise features almost exclusively through top-activating token lists or decoder weight vectors, leaving the higher-order co-occurrence structure shared across features largely unexamined. We introduce a graph-structured representation in which each SAE feature is modelled as a token co-occurrence graph: nodes are the tokens most frequent near strong activations, and edges connect pairs that co-occur within local context windows. A custom WL-style, frequency-binned graph kernel then provides a similarity measure over this structural space. Applied as a proof of concept to features from a large SAE trained on GPT-2 Small and probed with a synthetic mixed-domain corpus, our clustering recovers heuristic motif families (punctuation-heavy patterns, language and script clusters, and code-like templates) that are not recovered by clustering on decoder cosine similarity. A token-histogram baseline achieves higher overall purity, so the contribution of the graph view is complementary rather than dominant: it surfaces structural relationships that token-frequency and decoder-weight views alone do not capture. Cluster assignments are stable across graph-construction hyperparameters and random seeds.

### [245] [Process Matters more than Output for Distinguishing Humans from Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06524)
*Milena Rmus,Mathew D. Hardy,Thomas L. Griffiths,Mayank Agrawal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 CogCAPTCHA30：由30个认知任务组成的测试集，用过程级特征而非仅看最终表现来区分人类与机器；结果显示过程特征在输出匹配时仍能有效识别差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型和自主智能体进入线上环境，可靠区分人类与机器变得重要。传统方法主要关注输出是否像人，而认知科学提示应评估行为产生的过程，因此作者希望检验认知过程特征是否能作为更稳健的人机判别依据。

Method: 作者构建30项认知任务以诱发诊断性的过程级特征，并比较性能指标与过程特征的人机判别能力。实验对象包括前沿通用智能体、在人类决策数据上微调的模型 Centaur，以及基于 Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct 的动作级监督微调和过程级微调方法。

Result: 过程级特征比单纯任务表现提供更强判别信号，在输出匹配条件下平均分类 AUC 达到0.88。广泛的人类决策微调提升了类人过程表现，任务特定的过程级监督进一步增强了行为模仿，但跨任务迁移时优势减弱。

Conclusion: 显式过程级监督可提升机器的类人认知行为模仿，但前提是具备合适且任务相关的过程表征；过程规格化与可迁移性是实现机器类人认知过程的关键瓶颈。

Abstract: Reliable human-machine discrimination is becoming increasingly important as large language models and autonomous agents are deployed in online settings. Existing approaches evaluate whether a system can produce behavior or responses indistinguishable from those of a human, following the emphasis on outputs as a criterion for intelligence proposed by Alan Turing. Cognitive science offers an alternative perspective: evaluating the process by which behavior is produced. To test whether cognitive processes can reliably distinguish humans from machines, we introduce CogCAPTCHA30, a battery of 30 cognitive tasks designed to elicit diagnostic process-level features even when task performance is matched. Across the battery, process-level features provide stronger discriminative signal than performance metrics alone, reliably distinguishing humans from agents even under output matching (mean process-feature classifier AUC = 0.88). To evaluate agentic process differences, we compare off-the-shelf frontier agents (Claude Sonnet 4.5, GPT-5, Gemini 2.5 Pro), Centaur (a language model fine-tuned on 10.7M human decisions), and two task-specific fine-tuning approaches applied to Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct: action-level supervised fine-tuning (A-SFT) and process-level fine-tuning (P-SFT), which directly optimizes process features. Broad fine-tuning on human decisions improves human-like task processes relative to off-the-shelf agents, while task-specific process-level supervision further improves behavioral mimicry. However, this advantage diminishes under cross-task transfer when supervised process targets do not naturally generalize across tasks. Explicit process-level supervision can improve human behavioral mimicry, but only if appropriate task-specific process representations are available, highlighting process specification as a bottleneck for achieving human-like cognitive processes in machines.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构建 GlazyBench 数据集，收集 23,148 个真实釉料配方；定义两个核心任务：一是根据原材料配方预测烧成后的表面属性，如颜色、透明度等；二是基于这些属性生成釉面视觉图像。同时建立传统机器学习、大语言模型、深度生成模型和大型多模态模型等基线。

Conclusion: GlazyBench 为 AI 辅助材料设计，尤其是陶瓷釉料设计，开辟了新的研究方向，并提供了可用于系统评估模型性能的标准化基准。

Abstract: Developing ceramic glazes is a costly, time-consuming process of trial and error due to complex chemistry, placing a significant burden on independent artists. We propose GlazyBench, the first dataset for AI-assisted glaze design. Comprising 23,148 real glaze formulations, GlazyBench supports two primary tasks: predicting post-firing surface properties, such as color and transparency, from raw materials, and generating accurate visual representations of the glaze based on these properties. We establish comprehensive baselines for property prediction using traditional machine learning and large language models, alongside image generation benchmarks using deep generative and large multimodal models. Our experiments demonstrate promising yet challenging results. GlazyBench pioneers a new research direction in AI-assisted material design, providing a standardized benchmark for systematic evaluation.

### [247] [SpatialEpiBench: Benchmarking Spatial Information and Epidemic Priors in Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06530)
*Ruiqi Lyu,Alistair Turcan,Bryan Wilder*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 SpatialEpiBench，一个面向真实公共卫生场景的时空流行病预测基准，发现多数空间邻接信息模型在多种预测跨度上甚至弱于简单的 last-value baseline。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流行病预测对公共卫生响应、资源配置和暴发干预至关重要，但数据稀疏、噪声大且高度非平稳；同时，现有研究缺乏标准化时空预测基准，常用的简单时间划分评估也不符合实时滚动预测实践。

Method: 构建包含 11 个流行病数据集的 SpatialEpiBench，采用标准化滚动评估和暴发相关指标；评估结合地理邻接信息与常见流行病学先验的预测模型，并与简单 last-value baseline 在 1 天到 1 个月预测期上比较。

Result: 多数邻接信息驱动的时空预测方法在不同预测跨度、甚至暴发期间均不如 last-value baseline；研究识别出三类主要失败模式：暴发预判不足、难以处理稀疏与噪声、常见地理邻接难以有效表征流行病学空间关系。

Conclusion: 该工作强调当前时空流行病预测模型在真实操作场景中的局限，SpatialEpiBench 可作为更严格、更贴近实践的评测平台，推动发展真正具备公共卫生实用价值的预测模型。

Abstract: Accurate epidemic forecasting is crucial for public health response, resource allocation, and outbreak intervention, but remains difficult with sparse, noisy, and highly non-stationary data. Because epidemics unfold across interacting regions, spatiotemporal methods are natural candidates for improving forecasts. Despite growing interest in spatial information, no standardized benchmark exists, and current evaluations often use simple chronological train-test splits that do not reflect real-time forecasting practice. We address this gap with SpatialEpiBench, a challenging benchmark for spatiotemporal epidemic forecasting in realistic public-health settings. SpatialEpiBench includes 11 epidemic datasets with standardized rolling evaluations and outbreak-specific metrics. We evaluate adjacency-informed forecasting models with widely used epidemic priors that adapt general models to epidemiology, but find that most methods underperform a simple last-value baseline from 1 day to 1 month ahead, even during outbreaks and with these priors. We identify three major failure modes: (1) poor outbreak anticipation, (2) difficulty handling sparsity and noise, and (3) limited utility of common geographic adjacency for epidemiological spatial information. We release benchmark data, code, and instructions at https://github.com/Rachel-Lyu/SpatialEpiBench to support development of operationally useful epidemic forecasting models.

### [248] [Ex Ante Evaluation of AI-Induced Idea Diversity Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06540)
*Nafis Saami Azad,Raiyan Abdul Baten*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需人机交互数据的评估框架，用于提前衡量生成式AI在创意任务中可能导致的人类创意多样性下降与群体层面的“拥挤”风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有创意AI评估多关注个体产出质量或效用，但创意作品是在群体中被消费的；如果许多人产生相似想法，单个想法的价值会下降。因此，AI可能提升个体表现，却同时加剧群体层面的创意同质化，这构成现有评估的盲区。

Method: 作者将创意想法建模为具有拥挤性的资源，基于模型生成样本与匹配的无AI辅助人类基线进行分布内比较，提出过度拥挤系数Δ和相对人类多样性比率ρ，并给出ρ≥1作为无额外拥挤的平价条件；同时将Δ与一个包含曝光依赖冗余成本的采用博弈相连接。

Result: 在短故事、营销口号和替代用途任务中，三个前沿大语言模型在多种拥挤核设定下均低于平价水平，表明存在相对人类基线的额外拥挤风险；并且估计结果可在可行的模型样本规模下稳定。

Conclusion: AI诱导的创意多样性坍缩可以通过模型开发阶段的离线基准测试进行预先评估；同时，不同生成协议的实验表明，通过有针对性的设计可降低拥挤风险，使群体感知的创意AI评估成为可操作的开发目标。

Abstract: Creative AI systems are typically evaluated at the level of individual utility, yet creative outputs are consumed in populations: an idea loses value when many others produce similar ones. This creates an evaluation blind spot, as AI can improve individual outputs while increasing population-level crowding. We introduce a human-relative framework for benchmarking AI-induced human diversity collapse without requiring human-AI interaction data, providing an ex ante protocol to estimate crowding risk from model-only generations and matched unaided human baselines. By modeling ideas as congestible resources, we show that source-level crowding is identifiable from within-distribution comparisons, yielding an excess-crowding coefficient $Δ$ and a human-relative diversity ratio $ρ$. We show that $ρ\ge1$ is the no-excess-crowding parity condition and connect $Δ$ to an adoption game with exposure-dependent redundancy costs. Across short stories, marketing slogans, and alternative-uses tasks, three frontier LLMs fall below parity across crowding kernels. Estimates stabilize with feasible model-only sample sizes. Importantly, generation-protocol variants show that crowding can be reduced through targeted design, making diversity collapse an actionable, development-time evaluation target for population-aware creative AI.

### [249] [Improved techniques for fine-tuning flow models via adjoint matching: a deterministic control pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06583)
*Zhengyi Guo,Jiayuan Sheng,David D. Yao,Wenpin Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种用于流式生成模型偏好对齐的确定性伴随匹配框架，将对齐问题表述为速度场上的最优控制，并通过截断伴随降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型偏好对齐方法可能训练不稳定、计算代价高，且在提升偏好指标时容易损害多样性与模式覆盖；因此需要一种更稳定、可解释且高效的对齐框架。

Method: 将流式生成模型的人类偏好对齐建模为速度场最优控制问题；在当前策略下将控制量直接回归到由价值梯度诱导的目标；提出截断伴随方案，仅在轨迹终端段集中计算；并扩展到非标准 KL 正则以调节对齐强度和分布保持。

Result: 在 SiT-XL/2 和 FLUX.2-Klein-4B 上，方法在多个对齐指标上取得稳定提升，同时显著改善生成多样性与模式保持，并带来明显计算节省。

Conclusion: 该框架为流式生成模型偏好对齐提供了稳定、高效且灵活的最优控制视角，能在对齐效果、计算成本和分布保真之间取得更好的平衡。

Abstract: We propose a deterministic adjoint matching framework that formulates human preference alignment for flow-based generative models as an optimal control problem over velocity fields. One can directly regress the control toward a value-gradient-induced target under the current policy, leading to a simple and stable training objective. Building on this perspective, we introduce a truncated adjoint scheme that focuses computation on the terminal portion of the trajectory, where reward-relevant signals concentrate, which yields substantial computational savings while preserving alignment quality. We further generalize the framework beyond standard KL-based regularization, allowing more flexible trade-offs between alignment strength and distributional preservation. Experiments on SiT-XL/2 and FLUX.2-Klein-4B demonstrate consistent gains across multiple alignment metrics, along with substantially improved diversity and mode preservation.

</details>


### [250] [NeuroAgent: LLM Agents for Multimodal Neuroimaging Analysis and Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06584)
*Lujia Zhong,Yihao Xia,Jianwei Zhang,Shuo huang,Jiaxin Yue,Mingyang Xia,Yonggang Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NeuroAgent 是一个由大语言模型驱动的多智能体框架，用于自动化多模态神经影像预处理与下游分析，并在阿尔茨海默病分类任务中取得较高性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态神经影像数据（如 sMRI、fMRI、dMRI/DTI、PET）的预处理流程复杂、依赖模态特定工具链，且后续统计分析和疾病分类通常需要额外的任务代码、评估协议和数据格式转换，阻碍了从原始数据到可复现分析的高效衔接。

Method: 论文提出 NeuroAgent，采用层级式多智能体架构和反馈驱动的 Generate-Execute-Validate 引擎。系统通过自然语言解析用户意图，自动生成可执行预处理代码，执行后检测运行错误并尝试恢复，同时验证输出完整性；还支持 Human-In-The-Loop 机制处理需要人工审查的边界情况。

Result: 在 ADNI 全阶段共 1,470 名受试者数据上评估，其中包含 sMRI 和表格数据，并有部分受试者具备 Tau-PET、fMRI 和 DTI。消融实验显示强模型可达到最高 100% 的意图解析准确率，Qwen3.5-27B 达到 84.8% 的端到端预处理步骤正确率。基于自动预处理的四模态数据，阿尔茨海默病分类 AUC 达到 0.9518，优于所有单模态基线。

Conclusion: NeuroAgent 展示了利用 LLM 智能体降低神经影像预处理人工成本、提升多模态分析自动化和复现性的潜力，并可支持端到端的神经影像研究工作流。

Abstract: Multimodal neuroimaging analysis often involves complex, modality-specific preprocessing workflows that require careful configuration, quality control, and coordination across heterogeneous toolchains. Beyond preprocessing, downstream statistical analysis and disease classification commonly require task-specific code, evaluation protocols, and data-format conventions, creating additional barriers between raw acquisitions and reproducible scientific analysis. We present NeuroAgent, an LLM-driven agentic framework that automates key preprocessing and analysis steps for heterogeneous neuroimaging data, including sMRI, fMRI, dMRI, and PET, and supports interactive downstream analysis through natural-language queries. NeuroAgent employs a hierarchical multi-agent architecture with a feedback-driven Generate-Execute-Validate engine: agents autonomously generate executable preprocessing code, detect and recover from runtime errors, and validate output integrity. We evaluate the system on 1,470 subjects pooled across all ADNI phases (CN=1,000, AD=470), where all subjects have sMRI and tabular data, with subsets also having Tau-PET (n=469), fMRI (n=278), and DTI ($n=620$). Pipeline ablation studies across multiple LLM backends show that capable models reach up to 100% intent-parsing accuracy, with the strongest backend (Qwen3.5-27B) reaching 84.8% end-to-end preprocessing step correctness. Automated recovery limits manual intervention to edge cases where human review is required via the Human-In-The-Loop interface. For Alzheimer's Disease classification using automatically preprocessed multimodal data, our agent ensemble achieves an AUC of 0.9518 with four modalities, outperforming all single-modality baselines. These results show that NeuroAgent can reduce the manual effort required for neuroimaging preprocessing and enable end-to-end automated analysis pipelines for neuroimaging research.

### [251] [On Unbiased Parameter Estimation and Signal Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05276)
*Joonas Lahtinen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文将深度无偏源定位理论扩展到任意数量非零参数的无偏参数估计与信号重建，给出无噪声可恢复参数数量上界，并解释标准化/无偏方法的噪声鲁棒性及传感器数量与信噪比之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度无偏源定位理论主要面向特定源定位问题，而压缩感知、多源估计和成像重建中普遍关注“精确可重构性”。本文旨在从理论上回答任意多个非零参数何时可被无偏恢复，并解释标准化与无偏方法在噪声条件下表现稳健的原因。

Method: 作者建立无偏参数估计与信号重建的理论框架，在无噪声情形推导可恢复非零参数数量的上界；同时定义一种概率度量，用于评估恢复所有非零参数且保持正确幅值排序的概率，并结合数值实验验证理论结论。

Result: 理论上得到可恢复参数数量的上界，提出的概率度量能够刻画正确恢复及幅值排序的可能性；分析揭示了传感器数量与信噪比之间存在权衡关系。数值实验与理论发现一致。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了深度无偏源定位理论，为无偏估计、稀疏重建和多源成像中的精确可恢复性提供了数学解释，并阐明了方法鲁棒性与系统设计参数之间的关系。

Abstract: In this paper, we expand the theory of depth-unbiased source localization to unbiased parameter estimation and signal reconstruction of an arbitrary number of non-zero parameters to be recovered. The topic touches on the concept of exact reconstructibility, most commonly known in compressed sensing and multisource estimation in various imaging problems. The theoretical results derive upper bounds on the number of recoverable parameters in the noiseless case, and a probability measure is defined to assess the probability of obtaining all non-zero parameters with correct magnitude order. The work provides a mathematical explanation of the open question regarding the noise robustness of standardized and unbiased methods. Also, the paper reveals a trade-off between the number of sensors and the signal-to-noise ratio. Numerical experiments demonstrate the theoretical findings.

### [252] [When Semantic Communication Meets Queueing: Cross-Layer Latency and Task Fidelity Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05514)
*Yalin E. Sagduyu,Tugba Erpek*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究无线信道下的语义图像传输，通过动态调节潜在维度在语义精度、时延和信息新鲜度之间取得权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固定速率传输难以同时满足无线资源受限、任务推理精度和低时延更新需求。语义通信可只传递任务相关信息，但不同语义表示长度会影响信道占用、队列时延和任务准确率，因此需要在线自适应控制语义速率。

Method: 构建多任务语义自编码器，在块瑞利衰落与加性高斯白噪声信道上同时执行图像重构和标签预测；将潜在维度定义为跨层控制变量。进一步提出两类在线语义速率控制策略：基于漂移加惩罚的队列感知策略，在长期语义错误约束下最小化时延；以及面向信息年龄的策略，用于最小化时间平均AoI。

Result: 较大的潜在表示可提升推理准确率和语义保真度，但会增加服务时间、信道使用次数和排队时延。自适应语义速率控制相比固定速率基线能更有效利用频谱，并显著降低时延和AoI。

Conclusion: 语义表示维度可作为连接物理层资源与应用层任务质量的关键控制变量。通过根据拥塞状态和语义误差约束动态调整语义速率，系统能够在任务保真度、频谱效率、时延和信息新鲜度之间实现更优折中。

Abstract: Semantic communication (SemCom) with learned encoder-decoder architectures enables end-to-end learning of compact task-oriented representations optimized for the wireless channel, reducing channel resources needed to convey task-relevant information and improving spectrum efficiency. This paper studies semantic image transmission over block Rayleigh fading with AWGN using a multi-task semantic autoencoder that jointly reconstructs images and predicts labels from the received waveform. The latent dimension (complex channel uses per source sample) serves as a cross-layer control variable governing semantic fidelity and channel resource usage. We characterize the resulting latency-task fidelity tradeoff: larger latent representations improve inference accuracy but increase service time, channel uses, and queueing delay. Building on this insight, we develop online semantic-rate controllers that adapt the latent dimension per update under a long-term semantic error constraint. A queue-aware drift-plus-penalty policy minimizes delay subject to an average semantic error cap, while a complementary age-aware policy minimizes time-average Age of Information (AoI). By adapting the semantic rate to congestion and fidelity requirements, the proposed framework improves spectrum utilization and enables timely semantic updates with significantly lower delay and AoI than fixed-rate baselines.

It is worthy to mention that two classes of maximal entanglement EAQECCs with a negative or a high positive net rate are derived. Moreover, two classes of distance-optimal and dimension-optimal LRCs are also obtained.

### [254] [An Additive Approximation Scheme for Generating Dyadic Codings for the Outputs of an LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05837)
*Daniella Bar-Lev,Farzad Farnoud,Ryan Gabrys*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究在编码率约束下，用二叉树诱导的二进分布近似离散概率分布，并给出常数速率情形下的多项式时间加性近似方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散概率分布（如大语言模型的下一词元分布）在某些编码或隐写应用中需要被二进概率结构近似；核心需求是在满足指定信息率的同时，尽量降低近似分布与原分布之间的总变差距离，以控制统计可检测性。

Method: 作者将问题表述为基于二叉树的支持集划分与二进概率分配问题，目标是在给定编码率约束下最小化总变差距离；并针对常数速率区间设计了多项式时间的加性近似算法。

Result: 论文声称得到具有可证明保证的近最优二进分布近似方法；在常数速率 regime 下，该方法能以多项式时间达到加性近似精度。

Conclusion: 该工作为率受限的二进分布近似提供了理论化算法框架，并展示其在基于大语言模型的隐写场景中的潜在应用，其中编码率对应每个词元嵌入的信息比特数，总变差界用于约束统计可检测性。

Abstract: We study the problem of approximating a discrete probability distribution, such as the next-token distribution of a large language model, by a dyadic distribution induced by a binary tree under encoding rate constraints. The objective is to partition the support of the distribution and assign dyadic probabilities to minimize total variation distance while achieving a prescribed rate. We formulate this task as a tree-based partitioning problem and develop a polynomial-time additive approximation scheme for the rate-constrained setting in the constant-rate regime. Our results provide provable guarantees for near-optimal dyadic approximations and, as an application, yield a principled framework for LLM-based steganography, where the rate maps to bits of hidden information embedded per token and the total variation bound controls statistical detectability.

</details>


### [255] [Identification for Inverse Gaussian Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06103)
*Mohammad Javad Salariseddigh*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究逆高斯信道在分子通信场景下的识别容量，给出了确定性编码与峰值时间约束下的上下界，并表明在温和噪声正则条件下码本规模呈超指数增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逆高斯信道是流体环境中分子通信的重要基础模型，刻画携带信息的分子通过扩散与漂移到达接收端的首次到达时间。识别通信关注接收端判断某一消息是否被发送，其容量规律与传统传输容量不同，因此需要专门刻画其渐近码本增长。

Method: 文章在峰值时间约束下分析确定性编码方案，推导识别码本大小的下界与上界；并引入关于噪声分布即随机首次到达时间的温和正则性条件，用于刻画码字长度趋于无穷时的识别容量尺度。

Result: 核心结果表明，在该正则条件成立时，逆高斯信道的识别容量对应的码本规模随码字长度 n 呈超指数增长，形式约为 2^{(n log n)R}，其中 R 为编码率。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了逆高斯分子通信信道在识别任务下具有不同于常规指数级增长的容量行为，为分子通信中的识别编码理论提供了容量界与渐近尺度刻画。

Abstract: We derive lower and upper bounds on the identification capacity of inverse Gaussian channels, a fundamental model for molecular communications in fluid environments. The analysis considers deterministic encoding schemes under a peak time constraint and characterizes the asymptotic growth of codebook sizes. A central result reveals that, under a mild regularity condition on the noise, i.e., the stochastic first arrival time of an information-carrying molecule propagating via diffusion and drift to the receiver, the identification capacity exhibits super-exponential growth in the codeword length, $n,$ i.e., $\sim 2^{(n \log n)R},$ where $R$ is the coding rate.

</details>


### [256] [Locally Repairable Codes with Availability via Elliptic Function Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06182)
*Junjie Huang,Chang-An Zhao*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文利用普通椭圆曲线及椭圆函数域自同构群构造具有一个或两个恢复集的局部可修复码，得到多族新的最优或近最优码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作主要依赖最大超奇异椭圆曲线构造最优局部可修复码，曲线选择范围较窄。本文希望引入具有较多有理点的普通椭圆曲线，并为两个恢复集的情形建立更一般的构造机制，以提升码长、局部性和可用性的灵活性。

Method: 首先基于普通椭圆曲线的椭圆函数域构造具有一个或两个恢复集的局部可修复码；其次通过椭圆函数域的自同构群提出两恢复集局部可修复码的一般框架；最后设计新的方法来确定构造中所需的函数 e_i，并结合超奇异与普通椭圆曲线实例化该框架。

Result: 获得若干新的 q 元最优局部可修复码族，码长达到 O(q+2√q)，且局部性更灵活；同时得到多族具有两个恢复集的局部可修复码。特别地，构造出一族 q^2 元两恢复集局部可修复码，码长为 O(q^2+2q)，Singleton 缺陷为 O(2ℓ/(q^2+2q-8ℓ))，其中 ℓ || q+2 且 4ℓ<q。

Conclusion: 本文扩展了最优局部可修复码构造中可用椭圆曲线的范围，并为具有两个恢复集的局部可修复码提供了统一且可实现的构造框架，在分布式存储纠删码设计中具有理论价值。

Abstract: Locally repairable codes with availability have become essential components in modern large-scale distributed cloud storage systems and numerous other applications. In this paper, we focus on the construction of locally repairable codes with one or two recovering sets via elliptic function fields. Prior pioneering work by Li et al. (IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory, vol. 65, no. 1, 2019) and Ma and Xing (J. Comb. Theory Ser. A., vol. 193, 2023) employed maximal supersingular elliptic curves to obtain several optimal (classical) locally repairable codes. In contrast, we consider ordinary elliptic curves with many rational points. This approach yields several new families of \(q\)-ary optimal locally repairable codes with length \(O(q+2\sqrt{q})\) and flexible locality. Consequently, our work broadens the selection of curves available for the construction of optimal locally repairable codes.
  Furthermore, we present a general framework for constructing locally repairable codes with two recovering sets via automorphism groups of elliptic function fields. To realize this framework, we devise a novel construction for determining the functions \(e_i\) in the construction of locally repairable codes. By employing both supersingular and ordinary elliptic curves, we obtain several families of locally repairable codes with two recovering sets. In particular, we construct a family of \(q^2\)-ary locally repairable codes with two recovering sets, achieving length \(O(q^2+2q)\) and Singleton-defect \(O\!\left(\frac{2\ell}{q^2+2q-8\ell}\right)\), where \(\ell \mid\mid q + 2\) with \(4\ell < q\).

</details>


### [257] [Fluid Antenna Systems Enabling 6G HRLLC With Port Switching Delay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06275)
*Xusheng Zhu,Kai-Kit Wong,Hao Xu,Chenguang Rao,Hyundong Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究流体天线系统在超可靠低时延通信中的有限块长性能，揭示端口数量、切换时延与可靠性/速率/能效之间存在唯一最优配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体天线系统可通过天线位置可重构性在紧凑终端中获得空间分集，适合6G用户终端；但实际端口切换会引入时延和信令开销，在有限块长HRLLC场景下可能显著损害可靠性与时延性能，因此需要系统性建模与性能分析。

Method: 论文显式建模空间相关衰落、端口切换时延和有限块长编码的耦合影响，推导平均块错误率和平均可达速率的精确闭式表达式，并从理论上证明可靠性、可达速率和能效关于端口维度严格单峰，同时给出区分FAS相对固定位置天线是否有净收益的切换时延阈值。

Result: 分析表明，增加端口数量可提升分集增益，但会因端口切换线性减少有效块长，从而加剧有限块长惩罚；数值结果验证理论推导，并显示当切换时延低于所推导阈值时，FAS可获得显著HRLLC性能增益。

Conclusion: FAS在HRLLC中具有潜在优势，但其收益依赖于端口数量和切换时延的精细权衡；严格单峰性保证存在唯一最优端口配置，而显式时延阈值为实际系统设计提供了可操作准则。

Abstract: Fluid antenna systems (FAS) exploit antenna position reconfigurability to unlock massive spatial diversity within compact form factors, making them a promising enabler for 6G user terminals (UTs). However, practical port switching incurs latency and signaling overhead, which can be particularly detrimental to hyper-reliable low-latency communications (HRLLC) under finite blocklength operation. This paper investigates FASenabled HRLLC by explicitly capturing the coupled effects of spatial correlation, port switching delay, and finite blocklength coding. We derive exact closed-form expressions for the average block error rate (BLER) and average achievable rate over spatially correlated fading channels. The resulting analysis reveals a fundamental design trade-off: increasing the number of ports improves diversity but linearly reduces the effective blocklength, thereby intensifying finite-blocklength penalties. A key theoretical contribution is a rigorous proof that reliability, achievable rate, and energy efficiency are strictly unimodal in the port dimension, ensuring a unique optimal port configuration. Furthermore, we characterize an explicit switching-delay threshold that separates regimes where FAS yields net gains over fixed-position antenna (FPA) systems. Numerical results validate the analysis and show that substantial HRLLC performance gains are achievable when the switching latency remains below the derived bound.

</details>


### [258] [Affine Subcode Ensemble Decoding for Degeneracy-Aware Quantum Error Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06547)
*Leo Wursthorn,Jonathan Mandelbaum,Sisi Miao,Hedongliang Liu,Holger Jäkel,Stergios Koutsioumpas,Laurent Schmalen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出将经典仿射子码集成译码扩展到量子LDPC码，并结合过完备校验矩阵，以改善BP译码在简并情况下的收敛性和逻辑错误率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子LDPC码适合低开销容错量子计算，但其简并性会削弱置信传播（BP）译码的收敛性能，导致译码困难。作者希望通过缩小有效简并解的搜索空间来提升译码表现。

Method: 作者证明向稳定子码校验矩阵追加线性无关行可减少有效简并解搜索空间；在此基础上，将经典仿射子码集成译码方法推广到量子场景，并在每条译码路径中使用过完备矩阵。

Result: 在环面码和广义自行车码上的蒙特卡洛仿真表明，该方法能改善BP译码收敛性，并降低逻辑错误率。

Conclusion: 通过追加校验信息、采用量子仿射子码集成译码及过完备矩阵，可以有效缓解量子LDPC码BP译码中由简并性引起的问题，提升译码可靠性。

Abstract: Quantum low-density parity-check codes are promising candidates for low-overhead fault-tolerant quantum computing, but degeneracy is known to impair the convergence of belief-propagation (BP) decoding of these codes. In this work, we show that appending linearly independent rows to a check matrix of a stabilizer code can reduce the search space for a valid degenerate solution. Motivated by this, we extend the recently proposed affine subcode ensemble decoding technique from the classical to the quantum setting. Moreover, we employ overcomplete matrices for each decoding path. Monte-Carlo simulations on toric and generalized bicycle codes demonstrate improved convergence and reduced logical error rate.

</details>


### [259] [Generalized Skew Multivariate Goppa Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06580)
*Elena Berardini,Pranav Trivedi*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出基于多元 Ore 多项式理论的广义斜多元 Goppa 码，并给出其参数界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有广义斜 Goppa 码可进一步推广到多元非交换多项式框架；需要理解新码类与广义斜 Reed–Solomon 码之间的关系，并估计其维数与最小距离。

Method: 利用多元 Ore 多项式构造广义斜多元 Goppa 码；为广义斜 Goppa 码建立新的校验矩阵；在特定假设下证明其为广义斜 Reed–Solomon 码的子域子码；据此推导新码类的参数界。

Result: 广义斜 Goppa 码被包含为特例；在若干假设下，它们可表示为广义斜 Reed–Solomon 码的子域子码；论文给出了斜多元 Goppa 码的维数下界/界限及最小距离界。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了斜 Goppa 码理论，将其嵌入多元 Ore 多项式框架，并通过与斜 Reed–Solomon 码的联系为新码族参数分析提供了工具。

Abstract: We introduce Generalized Skew Multivariate Goppa codes relying on the theory of multivariate Ore polynomials. These codes contain, as a particular case, the Generalized Skew Goppa codes. By providing a new parity check matrix for the latter, we show that, under some hypotheses, they are subfield subcodes of Generalized Skew Reed--Solomon codes. This result turns out to be helpful to study the parameters of Skew Multivariate Goppa codes, for which we provide bounds on their dimension and minimum distance.

</details>
